function displayDockUserGreeting(welcomeStr, greetingSalutationFormat, greetingFirstLastFormat, login, register)
{
    var greetingString;
    var results = hasUserCookie();
    if (results)
    {

        if (greetingFirstLastFormat == "N")
        {
            greetingString = getUserLastName() + ' ' + getUserFirstName();
        }
        else
        {
            greetingString = getUserFirstName() + ' ' + getUserLastName();
        }

        if (greetingSalutationFormat == '1')
        {
            greetingString = getUserSalutation() + ' ' + greetingString;
        }
        else if (greetingSalutationFormat == '2')
        {
            greetingString = greetingString + ' ' + getUserSalutation();
        }

    	$('dock_loginDD').style.display = 'none';
    	$('dock_welcomeMsgDisplay').innerHTML = welcomeStr + " " + greetingString;
    	$('dock_welcomeMsgDisplay').style.display = 'inline-block';

        //document.write(welcomeStr + ' ' + greetingString);
    }
    else{
    	var loggedIn = document.cookie.match ( 'WatersLoginCookie=(.*?)(;|$)' );

		if(typeof(loggedIn)=='undefined'){
			loggedIn = false;
		}
		//alert("After get loginIn cookie");
		if (! loggedIn )
		{
	        if (window.location.href.indexOf('login.htm') != -1)
	        {
	            var redirectUrl = '/waters/home.htm';
	        }
	        else
	        {
	            var redirectUrl = escape(window.location.href);
	        }
	        try{
	        	//$('dock_loginLink').href = 'https://www.waters.com/waters/login.htm?redirectUrl=' + redirectUrl + '&locale=en_IN';
	        	//if (window.location.href.indexOf('login.htm') != -1)
	        	//{
	        		$('dock_loginLink').style.display = 'none';
	        		$('dock_loginLink').href = '/waters/login.htm?redirectUrl=';
	        		var noHttp = $('dock_loginLink').href;
	        		var hasHttp = noHttp.replace("http://", "https://");
	        		$('dock_loginLink').href = hasHttp  + redirectUrl;
	        	//}
	        	$('dock_loginLink').innerHTML = login + "/" + register;
				$('dock_loginLink').style.display = 'block';
				$('dock_loginDD').style.display = 'none';
				$('dock_loginOption1').style.display = 'none';
				$('dock_loginOption2').style.display = 'none'; 
				$('dock_welcomeMsg').style.background = 'none';
				
	        }
	        catch(e){
		        var logIn = document.getElementById("dock_loginLink");
		        logIn.href = '/waters/login.htm?redirectUrl=';
		        var hasHttp = logIn.replace("http://", "https://");
		        logIn.href = hasHttp + redirectUrl;
				logIn.innerHTML = "Login" + "/" + "Register";
			}
		}
    }
}

function submitDockSearchForm() {
	s = s_gi(omniture_account);
	s.linkTrackVars = 'prop32,eVar32,prop37,eVar37,prop44,eVar44,events';
          s.linkTrackEvents = 'event9';
          s.events = 'event9';
	var str = document.getElementById('dock_qtemp').value;
	s.eVar32 = s.prop32 = str;
          s.eVar37 = s.prop37 = 'Header';

	//var tempSearchFormVar = getDockSelectSearch();
	var tempSearchFormVar = "search_2";
	selectedForm = document.getElementById(tempSearchFormVar);
	if(tempSearchFormVar != false){
		selectedForm.q.value = encodeURIComponent(document.getElementById('dock_qtemp').value);
        var searchBucket = document.getElementById('dock_'+tempSearchFormVar + '_desc');
        s.eVar44 = s.prop44 = searchBucket.value;
   		s.tl(true, 'o', str);
	}
	else{
		$('dockSearchHeading').innerHTML = "<font color=red>" + "Select Search Area" + "</font>";
		//document.getElementById('dockSearchHeading').value = "Select Search Area";
	}

    if(tempSearchFormVar != false){
		selectedForm.submit();
    }
	return false;
}

function toggleDockSearchForm(){
	jQuery('#dockedSearchHoverContainer').toggle();
	jQuery('#searchIconBoundingSpan').toggleClass('active');
}

		jQuery.noConflict();
		//show/hide docked nav
		jQuery(window).scroll(function(e){
			if(jQuery(this).scrollTop() >=125){
				if(!jQuery("#docked-nav").hasClass('active')){
					jQuery("#docked-nav").addClass('active').stop().slideDown(100);					
				}
			} else {
				if(jQuery("#docked-nav").hasClass('active')){				
					jQuery("#docked-nav").removeClass('active').stop().slideUp(100);		

					
					//reset hamburger menu
					jQuery("#screenWrapper").animate({
						marginLeft: "0px",
						duration: 200				
					});												
					jQuery("#hamburger-menu").animate({
						width: 'hide',
						duration: 200
					});
				}
			};		
		});
		
		jQuery("#hamburgerLocale").click(function(e){
			jQuery(this).toggleClass("active");
			jQuery("#countryPopUpDisplayHamburger").toggle();
		});
		jQuery("#dock_welcomeMsgDisplay").click(function(e){
			jQuery(this).toggleClass("active");
			jQuery("#dock_loginDD").toggle();
		});

		jQuery("#docked-nav .expand").click(function(e){
// 			if (! jQuery("#hamburger-menu").is(":visible") ) {

// 			}
			
			jQuery("#hamburger-menu").animate({
				width: 'toggle',
				duration: 200
			});			
		});

', <!--
// ------------------------------------------------------------------------ //
// -- A function that sets the login link based on the WatersLoginCookie -- //
// ------------------------------------------------------------------------ //
setLoginLink = function()
{
	var loggedIn = document.cookie.match ( 'WatersLoginCookie=(.*?)(;|$)' );

		if(typeof(loggedIn)=='undefined'){
			loggedIn = false;
		}
		//alert("After get loginIn cookie");
		if (! loggedIn )
		{
	        if (window.location.href.indexOf('login.htm') != -1)
	        {
	            var redirectUrl = '/waters/home.htm';
	        }
	        else
	        {
	            var redirectUrl = escape(window.location.href);
	        }
	        try{
				$('loginLink').href = 'https://www.waters.com/waters/login.htm?redirectUrl=' + redirectUrl + '&locale=en_IN';
				$('loginLink').innerHTML = "Login" + "/" + "Register";
	        }
	        catch(e){
		        var logIn = document.getElementById("loginLink");
				logIn.href = 'https://www.waters.com/waters/login.htm?redirectUrl=' + redirectUrl + '&locale=en_IN';
				logIn.innerHTML = "Login" + "/" + "Register";
			}
		}
};


var $j = jQuery.noConflict();
function submitSearchForm() {
	s = s_gi(omniture_account);
	s.linkTrackVars = 'prop32,eVar32,prop37,eVar37,prop44,eVar44,events';
          s.linkTrackEvents = 'event9';
          s.events = 'event9';
	var str = document.getElementById('qtemp').value;
	s.eVar32 = s.prop32 = str;
          s.eVar37 = s.prop37 = 'Header';

    //var tempSearchFormVar = getSelectSearch();
    var tempSearchFormVar = "search_2";
	selectedForm = document.getElementById(tempSearchFormVar);
	if(tempSearchFormVar != false){
		selectedForm.q.value = encodeURIComponent(document.getElementById('qtemp').value);
        var searchBucket = document.getElementById(tempSearchFormVar + '_desc');
        s.eVar44 = s.prop44 = searchBucket.value;
   		s.tl(true, 'o', str);
	}
	else{
		$('searchHeading').innerHTML = "<font color=red>" + "Select Search Area" + "</font>";
		//document.getElementById('searchHeading').value = "Select Search Area";
	}

    if(tempSearchFormVar != false){
    	selectedForm.submit();
    	
    }
	return false;
}

/*WEB-OBSOLETE - removed header search options
function getSelectSearch() {

	for (var i=0; i < document.searchForm.searchOption.length; i++)
	   {
	   	if (document.searchForm.searchOption[i].checked)
	      {
	     	 return document.searchForm.searchOption[i].value;
	      	}
	   }
		return document.searchForm.searchOption[0].checked;
	
}
*/

function toggleDisplay(id, blockOnlyFlag){
   var elem = document.getElementById(id);
   if(!blockOnlyFlag){
       elem.style.display = (elem.style.display == 'none') ? 'block' : 'none';
   }else{
       elem.style.display = 'block';
   }

}
$j(document).ready(function(){
	$j('.topNav li').hoverIntent(showMM,hideMM);
	$j('.megaMenuNav .topMenuSecondary').hover(showMMSecondary,hideMMSecondary);
	function showMM(){ 
		var megamenu = $j(this).children('.megaMen);
		megamenu.addClass('hover');
		megamenu.children('.megaMenuNav').children().removeClass('hover');
		megamenu.children('.megaMenuNav').children('.topMenuSecondary:first-child').addClass('hover');
	}
	function hideMM(){ 
		var megamenu = $j(this).children('.megaMen);
		megamenu.removeClass('hover');
	}
	function showMMSecondary(){
		var parentUL = $j(this).parents('.megaMenuNav');
		parentUL.children('.topMenuSecondary').removeClass('hover');
		$j(this).addClass('hover');
	}
	function hideMMSecondary(){
		if(!$j(this).parents('.megaMenuNav').children().last()) {
			$j(this).removeClass('hover');
		}
	}
	$j('#loginRegisterLI').bind('mouseenter mouseleave', function() {
		$j('#loginDD').toggle();
	});
	
	
	//extend left column border if it's on the page
	var pageHeight = $j("#LeftNav").parentsUntil("row").next().height()+40;
	if($j("#LeftNav").height() < pageHeight) {
		$j("#LeftNav").height(pageHeight);
	};
	
	//deep linking for tab changes (not suported by IE7)
	if(Modernizr.hashchange) {
		//how many tabs? (divide in 2 to deal with tracking script nodes)
		var tabCollection = $j("#sectionTabs").children("li");			
		var tabLength = tabCollection.length;
		var selectedTab = window.location.hash;
		selectedTab = selectedTab.toUpperCase();
		//translate to the tab you want
		switch(selectedTab) {
	
			case "#S1":
				tabCollection.each( function(index) {
					str = $j(this).html();
					str = str.replace(/\s+/g, '');

					}
				});
				break;

function trackClick(reporting_pageName, link_analytics_prop52, link_analytics_prop53, link_analytics_prop54, link_analytics_prop55, link_analytics_prop57, link_analytics_prop58) {
	//handle the interaction here
	s = s_gi(omniture_account);
	s.linkTrackVars = 'prop51,prop52,prop53,prop54,prop55,prop56,prop57,prop58,eVar51,eVar52,eVar53,eVar54,eVar55,eVar56,eVar57,eVar58,events';
	s.linkTrackEvents = 'event52';
	s.events = 'event52';
	s.prop51 = s.eVar51 = reporting_pageName;
	s.prop52 = s.eVar52 = link_analytics_prop52;
	s.prop53 = s.eVar53 = link_analytics_prop53;
	s.prop54 = s.eVar54 = link_analytics_prop54;
	s.prop55 = s.eVar55 = link_analytics_prop55;
	s.prop57 = s.eVar57 = s.prop52 + ':' + s.prop53 + ':' + s.prop54 + ':' + s.prop55;
	s.prop58 = s.eVar58 = link_analytics_prop58;
	s.tl(this, 'o', 'megamen);
};
function trackTimer(s_prop61, s_prop62, s_prop63) {
	s = s_gi(omniture_account);
	s.linkTrackVars = 'prop61,prop62,prop63,eVar61,eVar62,eVar63,events';
	s.linkTrackEvents = 'event51';
	s.events = 'event51';
	s.prop61 = s.eVar61 = s_prop61;
	s.prop62 = s.eVar62 = s_prop62;
	s.prop63 = s.eVar63 = s_prop63;
	s.tl(true, 'o', 'mouseover');
};

	s.linkTrackEvents = 'event52';
	s.events = 'event52';
	s.prop51 = s.eVar51 = reporting_pageName;
	s.prop54 = s.eVar54 = "Promo";
	s.prop55 = s.eVar55 = link_analytics_prop55;
	s.prop58 = s.eVar58 = link_analytics_prop58;
	s.prop59 = s.eVar59 = link_analytics_prop59;
	s.prop60 = s.eVar60 = s.prop59 + ':' + s.prop55 + ':' + s.prop58;

};

function trackFeedClick(reporting_pageName, link_analytics_prop55,
		link_analytics_prop58, link_analytics_prop59){
	s = s_gi(omniture_account);

	s.prop58 = s.eVar58 = link_analytics_prop58;

	s.prop60 = s.eVar60 = s.prop59 + ':'+s.prop54+':' + s.prop55 + ':' + s.prop58;

function displayDockUserGreeting(welcomeStr, greetingSalutationFormat, greetingFirstLastFormat, login, register)
{
    var greetingString;
    var results = hasUserCookie();
    if (results)
    {

        if (greetingFirstLastFormat == "N")
        {
            greetingString = getUserLastName() + ' ' + getUserFirstName();
        }
        else
        {
            greetingString = getUserFirstName() + ' ' + getUserLastName();
        }

        if (greetingSalutationFormat == '1')
        {
            greetingString = getUserSalutation() + ' ' + greetingString;
        }
        else if (greetingSalutationFormat == '2')
        {
            greetingString = greetingString + ' ' + getUserSalutation();
        }

    	$('dock_loginDD').style.display = 'none';
    	$('dock_welcomeMsgDisplay').innerHTML = welcomeStr + " " + greetingString;
    	$('dock_welcomeMsgDisplay').style.display = 'inline-block';

        //document.write(welcomeStr + ' ' + greetingString);
    }
    else{
    	var loggedIn = document.cookie.match ( 'WatersLoginCookie=(.*?)(;|$)' );

		if(typeof(loggedIn)=='undefined'){
			loggedIn = false;
		}
		//alert("After get loginIn cookie");
		if (! loggedIn )
		{
	        if (window.location.href.indexOf('login.htm') != -1)
	        {
	            var redirectUrl = '/waters/home.htm';
	        }
	        else
	        {
	            var redirectUrl = escape(window.location.href);
	        }
	        try{
	        	//$('dock_loginLink').href = 'https://www.waters.com/waters/login.htm?redirectUrl=' + redirectUrl + '&locale=en_IN';
	        	//if (window.location.href.indexOf('login.htm') != -1)
	        	//{
	        		$('dock_loginLink').style.display = 'none';
	        		$('dock_loginLink').href = '/waters/login.htm?redirectUrl=';
	        		var noHttp = $('dock_loginLink').href;
	        		var hasHttp = noHttp.replace("http://", "https://");
	        		$('dock_loginLink').href = hasHttp  + redirectUrl;
	        	//}
	        	$('dock_loginLink').innerHTML = login + "/" + register;
				$('dock_loginLink').style.display = 'block';
				$('dock_loginDD').style.display = 'none';
				$('dock_loginOption1').style.display = 'none';
				$('dock_loginOption2').style.display = 'none'; 
				$('dock_welcomeMsg').style.background = 'none';
				
	        }
	        catch(e){
		        var logIn = document.getElementById("dock_loginLink");
		        logIn.href = '/waters/login.htm?redirectUrl=';
		        var hasHttp = logIn.replace("http://", "https://");
		        logIn.href = hasHttp + redirectUrl;
				logIn.innerHTML = "Login" + "/" + "Register";
			}
		}
    }
}

function submitDockSearchForm() {
	s = s_gi(omniture_account);
	s.linkTrackVars = 'prop32,eVar32,prop37,eVar37,prop44,eVar44,events';
          s.linkTrackEvents = 'event9';
          s.events = 'event9';
	var str = document.getElementById('dock_qtemp').value;
	s.eVar32 = s.prop32 = str;
          s.eVar37 = s.prop37 = 'Header';

	//var tempSearchFormVar = getDockSelectSearch();
	var tempSearchFormVar = "search_2";
	selectedForm = document.getElementById(tempSearchFormVar);
	if(tempSearchFormVar != false){
		selectedForm.q.value = encodeURIComponent(document.getElementById('dock_qtemp').value);
        var searchBucket = document.getElementById('dock_'+tempSearchFormVar + '_desc');
        s.eVar44 = s.prop44 = searchBucket.value;
   		s.tl(true, 'o', str);
	}
	else{
		$('dockSearchHeading').innerHTML = "<font color=red>" + "Select Search Area" + "</font>";
		//document.getElementById('dockSearchHeading').value = "Select Search Area";
	}

    if(tempSearchFormVar != false){
		selectedForm.submit();
    }
	return false;
}

function toggleDockSearchForm(){
	jQuery('#dockedSearchHoverContainer').toggle();
	jQuery('#searchIconBoundingSpan').toggleClass('active');
}

		//show/hide docked nav
		jQuery(window).scroll(function(e){
			if(jQuery(this).scrollTop() >=125){
				if(!jQuery("#docked-nav").hasClass('active')){

						width: 'hide',
						duration: 200
					});
				}
			};		
		});

', <!--
// ------------------------------------------------------------------------ //
// -- A function that sets the login link based on the WatersLoginCookie -- //
// ------------------------------------------------------------------------ //
setLoginLink = function()
{
	var loggedIn = document.cookie.match ( 'WatersLoginCookie=(.*?)(;|$)' );

		if(typeof(loggedIn)=='undefined'){
			loggedIn = false;
		}
		//alert("After get loginIn cookie");
		if (! loggedIn )
		{
	        if (window.location.href.indexOf('login.htm') != -1)
	        {
	            var redirectUrl = '/waters/home.htm';
	        }
	        else
	        {
	            var redirectUrl = escape(window.location.href);
	        }
	        try{
				$('loginLink').href = 'https://www.waters.com/waters/login.htm?redirectUrl=' + redirectUrl + '&locale=en_IN';
				$('loginLink').innerHTML = "Login" + "/" + "Register";
	        }
	        catch(e){
		        var logIn = document.getElementById("loginLink");
				logIn.href = 'https://www.waters.com/waters/login.htm?redirectUrl=' + redirectUrl + '&locale=en_IN';
				logIn.innerHTML = "Login" + "/" + "Register";
			}
		}
};


var $j = jQuery.noConflict();
function submitSearchForm() {
	s = s_gi(omniture_account);
	s.linkTrackVars = 'prop32,eVar32,prop37,eVar37,prop44,eVar44,events';
          s.linkTrackEvents = 'event9';
          s.events = 'event9';
	var str = document.getElementById('qtemp').value;
	s.eVar32 = s.prop32 = str;
          s.eVar37 = s.prop37 = 'Header';

    //var tempSearchFormVar = getSelectSearch();
    var tempSearchFormVar = "search_2";
	selectedForm = document.getElementById(tempSearchFormVar);
	if(tempSearchFormVar != false){
		selectedForm.q.value = encodeURIComponent(document.getElementById('qtemp').value);
        var searchBucket = document.getElementById(tempSearchFormVar + '_desc');
        s.eVar44 = s.prop44 = searchBucket.value;
   		s.tl(true, 'o', str);
	}
	else{
		$('searchHeading').innerHTML = "<font color=red>" + "Select Search Area" + "</font>";
		//document.getElementById('searchHeading').value = "Select Search Area";
	}

    if(tempSearchFormVar != false){
    	selectedForm.submit();
    	
    }
	return false;
}

/*WEB-OBSOLETE - removed header search options
function getSelectSearch() {

	for (var i=0; i < document.searchForm.searchOption.length; i++)
	   {
	   	if (document.searchForm.searchOption[i].checked)
	      {
	     	 return document.searchForm.searchOption[i].value;
	      	}
	   }
		return document.searchForm.searchOption[0].checked;
	
}

function toggleDisplay(id, blockOnlyFlag){
   var elem = document.getElementById(id);
   if(!blockOnlyFlag){
       elem.style.display = (elem.style.display == 'none') ? 'block' : 'none';
   }else{
       elem.style.display = 'block';
   }

}
$j(document).ready(function(){
	$j('.topNav li').hoverIntent(showMM,hideMM);
	$j('.megaMenuNav .topMenuSecondary').hover(showMMSecondary,hideMMSecondary);
	function showMM(){ 
		var megamenu = $j(this).children('.megaMen);
		megamenu.addClass('hover');
		megamenu.children('.megaMenuNav').children().removeClass('hover');
		megamenu.children('.megaMenuNav').children('.topMenuSecondary:first-child').addClass('hover');
	}
	function hideMM(){ 
		var megamenu = $j(this).children('.megaMen);
		megamenu.removeClass('hover');
	}
	function showMMSecondary(){
		var parentUL = $j(this).parents('.megaMenuNav');
		parentUL.children('.topMenuSecondary').removeClass('hover');
		$j(this).addClass('hover');
	}
	function hideMMSecondary(){
		if(!$j(this).parents('.megaMenuNav').children().last()) {
			$j(this).removeClass('hover');
		}
	}
	$j('#loginRegisterLI').bind('mouseenter mouseleave', function() {
		$j('#loginDD').toggle();
	});
	
	
	//extend left column border if it's on the page
	var pageHeight = $j("#LeftNav").parentsUntil("row").next().height()+40;

		$j("#LeftNav").height(pageHeight);
	};
	
	//deep linking for tab changes (not suported by IE7)

function trackClick(reporting_pageName, link_analytics_prop52, link_analytics_prop53, link_analytics_prop54, link_analytics_prop55, link_analytics_prop57, link_analytics_prop58) {
	//handle the interaction here
	s = s_gi(omniture_account);
	s.linkTrackVars = 'prop51,prop52,prop53,prop54,prop55,prop56,prop57,prop58,eVar51,eVar52,eVar53,eVar54,eVar55,eVar56,eVar57,eVar58,events';
	s.linkTrackEvents = 'event52';
	s.events = 'event52';
	s.prop51 = s.eVar51 = reporting_pageName;
	s.prop52 = s.eVar52 = link_analytics_prop52;
	s.prop53 = s.eVar53 = link_analytics_prop53;
	s.prop54 = s.eVar54 = link_analytics_prop54;
	s.prop55 = s.eVar55 = link_analytics_prop55;
	s.prop57 = s.eVar57 = s.prop52 + ':' + s.prop53 + ':' + s.prop54 + ':' + s.prop55;
	s.prop58 = s.eVar58 = link_analytics_prop58;
	s.tl(this, 'o', 'megamen);
};

};
